<Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
I have been here several times and never a single time I was let down. I usually order the 3 course menu ($60) including appetizer, pasta, and an entree. Yes the portion is smaller than a la carte, but neither my partner nor I felt we needed to order more. The Chef is also good at making soup. It‚Äôs so good I was seriously considering order a regular bowl.

Wine by glass is quite pricey, usually between $12-15/glass. We decided to go with a bottle that fits within the budget we are more comfortable with.

It‚Äôs a family owned restaurant so maybe that‚Äôs why it feels even more homier.  The paintings on the walls were painted by the mother of the chef.  It does get busy on the weekends. It‚Äôll make the whole dining experience even better if they can reduce the number of tables in the restaurant. Our table was really close to other tables it reminded me of my dining experience in Paris.< /review>

<Text>Delicious food, with a very pleasing aesthetic.

Update 4/5/18:
On second visit the dinner was fairly bland. The menu was ambitious, but the dishes lacked flavor. I had a chicken stuffed with feta and sun-dried tomato, and my girlfriend had a beef pasta, both seemed like they were salt deficient and the pasta was overcooked.

Our appetizers were also fairly ambitious, hers was a bitter greens salad with prosciutto and a duck egg in which the flavors didn't quite mix. Mine was a mandarin and fennel salad that had good flavor but was very limp.

The wine selection was great, and the cider was quite delicious.

We did not have any desserts because they were out of the panna cotta at 7pm. The other desserts looked like they could be good, but just weren't appealing to us.

I recommend the tacos con chorizo.
I picked up dinner for the fam to go and chose 4 different types, 20 tacos total. I was unhappy with the way they were served - on paper plates with foil on top, and not in a tray - but the tacos were very good, especially the chorizo.
As a taco enthusiast, I would eat here again, although I would still be torn between this place and other taco places in Gilroy.</Review>

I am a BIG chicken when it comes to dental work! <text>Came here for lunch and was very much pleased with my meal. I was not expecting for such a small place to pack a lot of punch.

I ordered the Cajun Fried Chicken Sando with a side of fries and a coke. Didn't have to wait long for the food to come out after ordering. The look of the sandwich was tantalizing. I absolutely loved the amount of chicken that was put in. Before digging in, the employee explained what the ingredients were and where they came from which I thought was very cool to know and was a nice touch in customer service. After taking that first bite, the first thing that caught my attention was the crunch of the panko crust covering the chicken. It was such a satisfying texture and the generous amount of Cajun seasoning added so much flavor. The slaw on top of the chicken added a sweetness that complemented the saltiness of the meat. Not too spicy, even with the jalape√±os mixed in. The bread held up very well too, it didn't get soggy or fall apart on me. Overall a very solid, very flavorful sandwich. The side of fries were delicious as well. Crispy and well seasoned.

I definitely recommend this place to anyone wanting to grab a great sandwich or just a great lunch overall. I will be coming back to this place some time for sure.</text></record>

<Time>1571134796200< /Time><rating>5<//rating>< Review>
Monument Wine and Spirits is a treasure to Concord. To find this kind of liquor store is just about impossible these days. If you are a connoisseur of fine Liquors or wine. This is the store you need to know about.

First of all this store has been here as long as I can remember. and that's 50 years. I don't know how long but over fifty. I was in there tonight looking at his incredible selection of different kinds of Liquors. I ended up reminiscing about all kinds of old memories because of all of the old alcohol's that I hadn't seen in so long. Drambuie Frangelico and 10 to 15 other ones that I haven't seen for so long. I was looking for a particular Brandy today I tried at someone's house and really liked it.  I hadn't been able to find it. Of course they had it. They have everything.  Any kind of whiskey you can think of,any kind of wine. They've got it. From $500 bottles of whiskey and. To 500+ bottles of wine.  And ofcourse the regular old Kentucky whiskey for $10. This liquor stores a treasure to Concord. So if you want to get yourself something extra special. Or a great gift for a close friend. Or just to pick up a six-pack of beer this place is the best in town. I cannot say enough about this place. So it's you haven't been you must go. Enjoys and boresck or chrees.<//Review>

< review>
Monument Wine and Spirits is a landmark on Monument Four Corners. What used to be a long time ago the only Street around and Oak Grove was the other one that's why they had the four corners title because it was the only four corners in Concord at one time. I think they built at Wine and Spirits shortly after that. It's been there the whole time I've been around. And yeah they have an excellent selection of wine whiskeys up to like $500 bottles of whiskey and I'm not as much of a wine drinker but I'm pretty sure they have the same kind of wine are expensive very good wines. Very great good selection of beer. People are always friendly the owners are very nice can actually speak to him and everything. Something I always enjoy. I'm very disappointed in the customer service that you get from Moe's hole in the wall liquor stores or 7-Elevens anywhere really people that are on in these places just don't care and I never even heard of customer service they no bartering. And they don't bother either. So I absolutely love this place I'm going there and talk to the guy and get whatever I want ask questions about anything about alcohol or wine and they know the answer or they can order it. So five stars for this landmark in Concord and should be always used by the neighbors locally or if you're looking for something extra special then you should check this place out cuz it has extra special stuff. And I think the community should support places like this. Big 5 Stars would give it 6 if I could</review>

< Review>
My dad worked here years ago and they still have pictures of him hanging on the wall. I wasn't really excited to eat there at first but my dad hadn't been in there for years, so we went and I was pleasantly surprised. The menu was great and the children's menu was perfect for my kids. The food was delicious and the waitress was awesome. The best thing about the visit was listening to Tom Petty while my dad reminisced on all the good old days at the Galley where he bartended at met tons of women and ate like a king! Thanks for exceeding all my expectations and for all the memories!< /Review>

< text>
This place has a pretty crazy bar scene. I came here with a date and after a few drinks we were pretty much gone and the bartender just kept them coming.

If you're looking for a great bar scene, definitely check this place out. I love that the bartenders are friendly, don't bother checking IDs, and will pour a mean stiff drink. There's a lot to see and take in just at the bar - people hooking up, making out, or just plain getting wasted. It's a fun time especially if you've already had a few drinks.

We hung out for a while and then made our way back to the car. Luckily, they have a lot directly behind the restaurant and parking isn't that much. If you're looking to just hang out and have a few drinks, this place isn't bad. They also have a restaurant area  as well but I've only been to the bar.< /text>

<user_name>Copper Bear<//user_name><time>1494201340746<//time>< rate>
2< /rate>
< text>
Well... it looks cool and fun inside, but I can't say a lot more.  The food is ridiculously over priced for what you get.  I had the salmon and my girlfriend had the seared tuna.  $26 each.  I'm a terrible cook but I feel I could have managed what the gave us.

The tuna looked like and over-beat piece of sad grilled chicken when is came out. Resembling something that might come out of a hospital cafeteria. It was very over-cooked, which was a good thing since my girlfriend was afraid she might get sick from eating it.

My salmon was a good piece of fish, but I don't think they did anything other than cook it.  I like pretty boring food, but it and the broccoli were too boring even for me.

My girlfriend's Moscow mule was $13 and I just had water.  $65 and I can't understand why.  When we asked for the check they seemed surprised that we didn't want dessert, but my thought was it would probably be $26 for a mediocre brownie.

I will say our server, Erica, was very friendly.

I guess it's a staple of the area, but save your money.  Get a drink at the bar and enjoy the fun decor, but eat somewhere else.<//text>

(Translated by Google) We had reserved a table. But on our arrival there was no table available for us - just an alternative at a bar table or outside (where it was not so warm anymore). The interior of the restaurant is decorated with thousands of colored lights, which looks very kitschy but matches well with the rest. The service was friendly but we could not shake the feeling that it was just a courtesy. As an appetizer we got warm crusty bread and butter served - that was delicious. At the main course we were very disappointed. The rib eyes were very sinewy and the meat was badly parried. In addition, it tasted like nothing. The fries were mushy and the broccoli was still too hard (I like the vegetables crisp and not overcooked but that was still too raw). In the end it took forever until the plates were cleared and the bill came. All in all, the visit was very disappointing that the restaurant should be a "steakhouse" and the prices are also medium high. Therefore, we consider the current average rating of 4 points to be completely overvalued. As a place to have a drink in the evening at the bar and maybe a small snack / appetizer to eat, we would recommend it more.
